    40→let audioCtx = null;

    42→function getAudioContext() {
    43→  if (!audioCtx) {
    44→    audioCtx = new (window.AudioContext || window.webkitAudioContext)();
    45→  }
    46→  if (audioCtx.state === 'suspended') {
    47→    audioCtx.resume();
    48→  }
    49→  return audioCtx;
    50→}
    51→
    52→// Prime the AudioContext on first user interaction so it's ready for hands-free sends
    53→function primeAudio() {
    54→  try { getAudioContext(); } catch (_) {}
    55→}
    56→
    57→function _playTone(ctx, frequency, startTime, duration, gain) {
    58→  const osc  = ctx.createOscillator();
    59→  const amp  = ctx.createGain();
    60→  osc.connect(amp);
    61→  amp.connect(ctx.destination);
    62→  osc.type = 'sine';
    63→  osc.frequency.setValueAtTime(frequency, startTime);
    64→  amp.gain.setValueAtTime(0, startTime);
    65→  amp.gain.linearRampToValueAtTime(gain, startTime + 0.01);
    66→  amp.gain.exponentialRampToValueAtTime(0.001, startTime + duration);
    67→  osc.start(startTime);
    68→  osc.stop(startTime + duration);
    69→}
    70→
    71→function playSuccessSound() {
    72→  // Prefer speech synthesis — "Got it" is immediately understood
    73→  if ('speechSynthesis' in window) {
    74→    const utt = new SpeechSynthesisUtterance('Got it');
    75→    utt.rate   = 1.1;
    76→    utt.pitch  = 1.1;
    77→    utt.volume = 1;
    78→    window.speechSynthesis.speak(utt);
    79→    return;
    80→  }
    81→  // Fallback: ascending double chime
    82→  try {
    83→    const ctx = getAudioContext();
    84→    const now = ctx.currentTime;
    85→    _playTone(ctx, 880,  now,        0.22, 0.30); // A5
    86→    _playTone(ctx, 1320, now + 0.18, 0.38, 0.25); // E6
    87→  } catch (e) {
    88→    console.warn('Audio playback failed:', e);
    89→  }
    90→}
    91→
    92→function playFailureSound() {
    93→  // Descending dissonant triple-tone — distinct "uh-oh" signal
    94→  try {
    95→    const ctx = getAudioContext();
    96→    const now = ctx.currentTime;
    97→    _playTone(ctx, 330, now,        0.18, 0.40); // E4
    98→    _playTone(ctx, 262, now + 0.15, 0.18, 0.40); // C4
    99→    _playTone(ctx, 196, now + 0.30, 0.45, 0.35); // G3
   100→  } catch (e) {
   101→    console.warn('Audio playback failed:', e);
   102→  }
   103→}

   112→
   113→if (!SpeechRecognition) {

   121→function initRecognition() {
   122→  recognition = new SpeechRecognition();
   123→  recognition.continuous     = true;
   124→  recognition.interimResults = true;
   125→  recognition.lang           = navigator.language || 'en-US';
   126→  recognition.maxAlternatives = 1;
   127→
   128→  recognition.onstart = () => {
   129→    isListening = true;
   130→    finalTranscript = '';
   131→    interimText = '';
   132→    setRecordingUI(true);
   133→  };
   134→
   135→  recognition.onresult = (event) => {
   136→    let interim = '';
   137→    for (let i = event.resultIndex; i < event.results.length; i++) {
   138→      const result = event.results[i];
   139→      if (result.isFinal) {
   140→        finalTranscript += result[0].transcript + ' ';
   141→      } else {
   142→        interim += result[0].transcript;
   143→      }
   144→    }
   145→    interimText = interim;
   146→    const displayText = (finalTranscript + interim).trim();
   147→    updateLiveText(displayText);
   148→
   149→    // Reset silence timer on every result
   150→    resetSilenceTimer();
   151→  };
   152→
   153→  recognition.onerror = (event) => {
   154→    // 'no-speech' is common and expected — just stop cleanly
   155→    if (event.error !== 'no-speech') {
   156→      console.warn('Speech recognition error:', event.error);
   157→    }
   158→    stopListening();
   159→  };
   160→
   161→  recognition.onend = () => {
   162→    // onend fires when recognition stops for any reason
   163→    if (isListening) {
   164→      // We didn't call stop manually yet; auto-stop happened
   165→      finishRecording();
   166→    }
   167→  };
   168→}
   169→
   170→function resetSilenceTimer() {
   171→  clearTimeout(silenceTimer);
   172→  silenceTimer = setTimeout(() => {
   173→    if (isListening) stopListening();
   174→  }, SILENCE_DELAY);
   175→}
   176→
   177→/* ===== Recording controls ===== */
   178→function startListening() {
   179→  if (!recognition || isListening) return;
   180→  hideTranscriptBar();
   181→
   182→  // Ensure wake recognition is stopped before starting main recording
   183→  if (wakeMode) stopWakeRecognition();
   184→
   185→  try {
   186→    recognition.start();
   187→  } catch (e) {
   188→    console.warn('Could not start recognition:', e);
   189→    // Re-init in case of invalid state
   190→    initRecognition();
   191→    try { recognition.start(); } catch (_) {}
   192→  }
   193→
   194→  resetSilenceTimer();
   195→}
   196→
   197→function stopListening() {
   198→  clearTimeout(silenceTimer);
   199→  isListening = false; // mark before calling stop so onend doesn't re-trigger finishRecording
   200→  if (recognition) {
   201→    try { recognition.stop(); } catch (_) {}
   202→  }
   203→  finishRecording();
   204→}
   205→
   206→function finishRecording() {
   207→  setRecordingUI(false);
   208→  const text = finalTranscript.trim();
   209→  if (text) {
   210→    if (wakeTriggeredRecording) {
   211→      // Hands-free path: auto-send without requiring a tap
   212→      sendMessage(text);
   213→    } else {
   214→      showTranscriptBar(text);
   215→    }
   216→  }
   217→  wakeTriggeredRecording = false;
   218→  // Resume passive wake word listening if mode is active
   219→  if (wakeMode) scheduleWakeRestart();
   220→  updateWakeHint();
   221→}
   222→
   223→/* ===== UI state helpers ===== */

   225→  micBtn.classList.toggle('recording', recording);
   226→  micRing.classList.toggle('recording', recording);
   227→  micBtn.setAttribute('aria-pressed', recording ? 'true' : 'false');
   228→  micBtn.setAttribute('aria-label', recording ? 'Stop recording' : 'Start recording');
   229→  micHint.textContent = recording ? 'Tap to stop' : (wakeMode ? 'Say "Hey Chill" or tap' : 'Tap to speak');
   230→  micHint.classList.toggle('active', recording);
   231→  liveTranscript.hidden = !recording;
   232→  if (!recording) {
   233→    liveText.textContent = 'Listening…';
   234→    liveText.classList.remove('has-text');
   235→  }
   236→}
   237→
   238→function updateLiveText(text) {

   240→    liveText.textContent = text;
   241→    liveText.classList.add('has-text');
   242→  } else {
   243→    liveText.textContent = 'Listening…';
   244→    liveText.classList.remove('has-text');
   245→  }
   246→}
   247→

   252→
   253→function hideTranscriptBar() {

   258→/* ===== Mic button click (toggle) ===== */

   282→/* ===== Webhook send ===== */
   283→async function sendMessage(text) {
   284→  const webhookUrl = localStorage.getItem('webhookUrl') || '';
   285→  const timestamp  = new Date().toISOString();
   286→  const payload    = { text, source: 'hey-chill', timestamp };
   287→
   288→  // Add message to history immediately
   289→  const msgEl = addMessage(text, timestamp, 'sending');
   290→
   291→  if (!webhookUrl) {
   292→    updateMessageStatus(msgEl, 'no-webhook');
   293→    return;
   294→  }
   295→
   296→  try {
   297→    const res = await fetch(webhookUrl, {
   298→      method: 'POST',
   299→      headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
   300→      body: JSON.stringify(payload),
   301→    });
   302→    if (!res.ok) throw new Error(`HTTP ${res.status}`);
   303→    updateMessageStatus(msgEl, 'sent');
   304→    playSuccessSound();
   305→  } catch (err) {
   306→    console.warn('Webhook error:', err);
   307→    updateMessageStatus(msgEl, 'error');
   308→    playFailureSound();
   309→  }
   310→}
   311→
   312→/* ===== Message history ===== */
   313→function addMessage(text, timestamp, status) {
   314→  // Hide empty state
   315→  messagesEmpty.style.display = 'none';
   316→
   317→  const el = document.createElement('div');
   318→  el.className = `message ${status}`;
   319→
   320→  const timeStr = new Date(timestamp).toLocaleTimeString([], {
   321→    hour: '2-digit',
   322→    minute: '2-digit',
   323→  });
   324→
   325→  const statusLabel = {
   326→    sending:    'Sending…',
   327→    sent:       'Sent',
   328→    error:      'Failed',
   329→    'no-webhook': 'No webhook',
   330→  };
   331→
   332→  el.innerHTML = `
   333→    <p class="message-text">${escapeHtml(text)}</p>
   334→    <div class="message-meta">
   335→      <span class="message-time">${timeStr}</span>
   336→      <span class="message-status">${statusLabel[status] || status}</span>
   337→    </div>
   338→  `;
   339→
   340→  messagesEl.appendChild(el);
   341→  el.scrollIntoView({ behavior: 'smooth', block: 'end' });
   342→  return el;
   343→}
   344→
   345→function updateMessageStatus(el, status) {
   346→  el.className = `message ${status}`;
   347→  const statusEl = el.querySelector('.message-status');
   348→  const labels = {
   349→    sent:         'Sent',
   350→    error:        'Failed',
   351→    'no-webhook': 'No webhook set',
   352→  };
   353→  if (statusEl) statusEl.textContent = labels[status] || status;
   354→}
   355→
   356→function escapeHtml(str) {
   357→  return str
   358→    .replace(/&/g, '&amp;')
   359→    .replace(/</g, '&lt;')
   360→    .replace(/>/g, '&gt;')
   361→    .replace(/"/g, '&quot;')
   362→    .replace(/'/g, '&#39;');
   363→}

   388→function closeSettings() {

   392→/* ===== Wake Word Detection ===== */
   393→
   394→function isWakePhrase(transcript) {
   395→  return WAKE_PHRASES.some(phrase => transcript.includes(phrase));
   396→}
   397→
   398→function initWakeRecognition() {
   399→  wakeRecognition = new SpeechRecognition();
   400→  wakeRecognition.continuous     = true;
   401→  wakeRecognition.interimResults = true;
   402→  wakeRecognition.lang           = navigator.language || 'en-US';
   403→  wakeRecognition.maxAlternatives = 1;
   404→
   405→  wakeRecognition.onresult = (event) => {
   406→    for (let i = event.resultIndex; i < event.results.length; i++) {
   407→      const transcript = event.results[i][0].transcript.toLowerCase().trim();
   408→      if (isWakePhrase(transcript)) {
   409→        handleWakeWordDetected();
   410→        return;
   411→      }
   412→    }
   413→  };
   414→
   415→  wakeRecognition.onerror = (event) => {
   416→    if (event.error === 'not-allowed' || event.error === 'service-not-allowed') {
   417→      // Microphone access denied — silently disable wake mode
   418→      disableWakeMode();
   419→      return;
   420→    }
   421→    if (wakeMode && !isListening && !wakeTriggered) {
   422→      scheduleWakeRestart();
   423→    }
   424→  };
   425→
   426→  wakeRecognition.onend = () => {
   427→    // Chrome stops continuous recognition periodically — restart unless we
   428→    // deliberately stopped it to hand off to main recording.
   429→    if (wakeMode && !isListening && !wakeTriggered) {
   430→      scheduleWakeRestart();
   431→    }
   432→  };
   433→}
   434→
   435→function startWakeRecognition() {
   436→  if (!wakeRecognition) initWakeRecognition();
   437→  wakeTriggered = false;
   438→  micRing.classList.add('listening-passive');
   439→  try {
   440→    wakeRecognition.start();
   441→  } catch (e) {
   442→    // InvalidStateError when already started — reinit and retry
   443→    initWakeRecognition();
   444→    try { wakeRecognition.start(); } catch (_) {}
   445→  }
   446→}
   447→
   448→function stopWakeRecognition() {
   449→  micRing.classList.remove('listening-passive');
   450→  if (wakeRecognition) {
   451→    try { wakeRecognition.stop(); } catch (_) {}
   452→  }
   453→}
   454→
   455→function scheduleWakeRestart() {
   456→  clearTimeout(wakeRestartTimer);
   457→  wakeRestartTimer = setTimeout(() => {
   458→    if (wakeMode && !isListening && !wakeTriggered) {
   459→      startWakeRecognition();
   460→    }
   461→  }, 300);
   462→}
   463→
   464→function handleWakeWordDetected() {
   465→  if (isListening || wakeTriggered) return;
   466→  wakeTriggered = true;
   467→  wakeTriggeredRecording = true; // flag so finishRecording auto-sends
   468→  stopWakeRecognition();
   469→  // Give the recognition engine a moment to fully stop before starting main recording
   470→  setTimeout(() => {
   471→    wakeTriggered = false;
   472→    startListening();
   473→  }, 250);
   474→}
   475→
   476→function enableWakeMode() {
   477→  wakeMode = true;
   478→  wakeBtn.classList.add('wake-active');
   479→  wakeBtn.setAttribute('aria-pressed', 'true');
   480→  wakeBtn.setAttribute('aria-label', 'Disable wake word');
   481→  wakeBtn.title = 'Wake word: ON';
   482→  localStorage.setItem('wakeMode', '1');
   483→  updateWakeHint();
   484→  if (!isListening) startWakeRecognition();
   485→}
   486→
   487→function disableWakeMode() {
   488→  wakeMode = false;
   489→  wakeBtn.classList.remove('wake-active');
   490→  wakeBtn.setAttribute('aria-pressed', 'false');
   491→  wakeBtn.setAttribute('aria-label', 'Enable wake word');
   492→  wakeBtn.title = 'Wake word: Hey Chill';
   493→  localStorage.setItem('wakeMode', '0');
   494→  clearTimeout(wakeRestartTimer);
   495→  stopWakeRecognition();
   496→  updateWakeHint();
   497→}
   498→
   499→function updateWakeHint() {
   500→  if (!isListening) {
   501→    micHint.textContent = wakeMode ? 'Say "Hey Chill" or tap' : 'Tap to speak';
   502→  }
   503→}
   504→
   505→wakeBtn.addEventListener('click', () => {
   506→  primeAudio();
   507→  if (wakeMode) {
   508→    disableWakeMode();
   509→  } else {
   510→    enableWakeMode();
   511→  }
   512→});
   513→
   514→// Restore wake mode preference across sessions
   515→if (SpeechRecognition && localStorage.getItem('wakeMode') === '1') {
   516→  enableWakeMode();
   517→}
   518→

   method: 'POST',\n      headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },\n      body: JSON.stringify(payload),\n    });\n    if (!res.ok) throw new Error(`HTTP ${res.status}`);\n }\n}\n\n/* ===== Message history ===== */\nfunction addMessage(text, timestamp, status) {\n  // Hide empty state\n  messagesEmpty.style.display = 'none';\n\n  const el = // mark before calling stop so onend doesn't re-trigger finishRecording\n  if (recognition) {\n    try { recognition.stop(); } catch (_) {}\n  }\n  finishRecording();\n}\n\nfunction finishRecording() {\n  const mode = activeMode;\n  setRecordingUI(false, mode);\n  const text = finalTranscript.trim();\n  brainstormAccumulator = '';\n  activeMode = null;\n  if (text) {\n    if (wakeTriggeredRecording) {\n      // Hands-free path: auto-send without requiring a tap\n      sendMessage(text);\n    } else {\n      showTranscriptBar(text);\n    }\n  }\n  wakeTriggeredRecording = false;\n  // Resume passive wake word listening if mode is active\n  if (wakeMode) scheduleWakeRestart();\n  updateWakeHint();\n}\n\n/* ===== UI state helpers ===== */\nfunction setRecordingUI(recording, mode) {\n  const quickActive      = recording && mode === 'quick';\n  const brainstormActive = recording && mode === 'brainstorm';\n\n  // Quick button\n  quickBtn.classList.toggle('recording', quickActive);\n  quickRing.classList.toggle('recording', quickActive);\n  quickBtn.setAttribute('aria-pressed', quickActive ? 'true' : 'false');\n  quickBtn.setAttribute('aria-label', quickActive ? 'Stop recording' : 'Quick Request \u2013 tap to speak');\n\n  // Brainstorm button\n  brainstormBtn.classList.toggle('recording', brainstormActive);\n  brainstormRing.classList.toggle('recording', brainstormActive);\n  brainstormBtn.setAttribute('aria-pressed', brainstormActive ? 'true' : 'false');\n  brainstormBtn.setAttribute('aria-label', brainstormActive ? 'Stop brainstorm recording' : 'Brainstorm \u2013 tap for continuous recording');\n\n  // Shared hint\n  if (quickActive) {\n    micHint.textContent = 'Listening\u2026 tap Quick to stop';\n    micHint.classList.add('active');\n    micHint.classList.remove('brainstorm-active');\n  } else if (brainstormActive) {\n    micHint.textContent = 'Recording\u2026 tap Brainstorm to stop';\n    micHint.classList.add('active', 'brainstorm-active');\n  } else {\n    micHint.classList.remove('active', 'brainstorm-active');\n    updateWakeHint();\n  }\n\n  liveTranscript.hidden = !recording;\n  if (!recording) {\n    liveText.textContent = 'Listening\u2026';\n    liveText.classList.remove('has-text');\n  }\n}\n\nfunction updateLiveText(text) {\n  if (text) {\n    liveText.textContent = text;\n    liveText.classList.add('has-text');\n  } else {\n    liveText.textContent = 'Listening\u2026';\n    liveText.classList.remove('has-text');\n  }\n}\n\nfunction showTranscriptBar(text) {\n  transcriptText.textContent = text;\n  transcriptBar.hidden = false;\n}\n\nfunction hideTranscriptBar() {\n  transcriptBar.hidden = true;\n  transcriptText.textContent = '';\n}\n\n/* ===== Button click handlers ===== */\nquickBtn.addEventListener('click', () => {\n  primeAudio();\n  if (isListening && activeMode === 'quick') {\n    stopListening();\n  } else if (!isListening) {\n    wakeTriggeredRecording = false; // manual tap \u2014 show transcript bar after\n    startListening('quick');\n  }\n});\n\nbrainstormBtn.addEventListener('click', () => {\n  primeAudio();\n  if (isListening && activeMode === 'brainstorm') {\n    stopListening();\n  } else if (!isListening) {\n    wakeTriggeredRecording = false;\n    startListening('brainstorm');\n  }\n});\n\n/* ===== Send / Discard ===== */\nsendBtn.addEventListener('click', async () => {\n  primeAudio();\n  const text = transcriptText.textContent.trim();\n  if (!text) return;\n  hideTranscriptBar();\n  await sendMessage(text);\n});\n\ndiscardBtn.addEventListener('click', () => {\n  hideTranscriptBar();\n});\n\n/* ===== Webhook send ===== */\nasync function sendMessage(text) {\n  const webhookUrl = localStorage.getItem('webhookUrl') || '';\n  const timestamp  = new Date().toISOString();\n  const payload    = { text, source: 'hey-chill', timestamp };\n\n  // Add message to history immediately\n  const msgEl = addMessage(text, timestamp, 'sending');\n\n  if (!webhookUrl) {\n    updateMessageStatus(msgEl, 'no-webhook');\n    return;\n  }\n\n  try {\n    const res = await fetch(webhookUrl, {\n      method: 'POST',\n      headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },\n      body: JSON.stringify(payload),\n    });\n    if (!res.ok) throw new Error(`HTTP ${res.status}`);\n    updateMessageStatus(msgEl, 'sent');\n    playSuccessSound();\n  } catch (err) {\n    console.warn('Webhook error:', err);\n    updateMessageStatus(msgEl, 'error');\n    playFailureSound();\n  }\n}\n\n/* ===== Message history ===== */\nfunction addMessage(text, timestamp, status) {\n  // Hide empty state\n  messagesEmpty.style.display = 'none';\n\n  const el = document.createElement('div');\n  el.className = `message ${status}`;\n\n  const timeStr = new Date(timestamp).toLocaleTimeString([], {\n    hour: '2-digit',\n    minute: '2-digit',\n  });\n\n  const statusLabel = {\n    sending:    'Sending\u2026',\n    sent:       'Sent',\n    error:      'Failed',\n    'no-webhook': 'No webhook',\n  };\n\n  el.innerHTML = `\n    <p class=\"message-text\">${escapeHtml(text)}</p>\n    <div class=\"message-meta\">\n      <span class=\"message-time\">${timeStr}</span>\n      <span class=\"message-status\">${statusLabel[status] || status}</span>\n    </div>\n  `;\n\n  messagesEl.appendChild(el);\n  el.scrollIntoView({ behavior: 'smooth', block: 'end' });\n  return el;\n}\n\nfunction updateMessageStatus(el, status) {\n  el.className = `message ${status}`;\n  const statusEl = el.querySelector('.message-status');\n  const labels = {\n    sent:         'Sent',\n    error:        'Failed',\n    'no-webhook': 'No webhook set',\n  };\n  if (statusEl) statusEl.textContent = labels[status] || status;\n}\n\nfunction escapeHtml(str) {\n  return str\n    .replace(/&/g, '&amp;')\n    .replace(/</g, '&lt;')\n    .replace(/>/g, '&gt;')\n    .replace(/\"/g, '&quot;')\n    .replace(/'/g, '&#39;');\n}\n\n/* ===== Settings modal ===== */\nsettingsBtn.addEventListener('click', openSettings);\nmodalClose.addEventListener('click',  closeSettings);\nmodalOverlay.addEventListener('click', (e) => {\n  if (e.target === modalOverlay) closeSettings();\n});\n\ndocument.addEventListener('keydown', (e) => {\n  if (e.key === 'Escape') closeSettings();\n});\n\nsaveSettings.addEventListener('click', () => {\n  const url = webhookInput.value.trim();\n  localStorage.setItem('webhookUrl', url);\n  closeSettings();\n});\n\nfunction openSettings() {\n  webhookInput.value = localStorage.getItem('webhookUrl') || '';\n  modalOverlay.hidden = false;\n  webhookInput.focus();\n}\n\nfunction closeSettings() {\n  modalOverlay.hidden = true;\n}\n\n/* ===== Wake Word Detection ===== */\n\nfunction isWakePhrase(transcript) {\n  return WAKE_PHRASES.some(phrase => transcript.includes(phrase));\n}\n\nfunction initWakeRecognition() {\n  wakeRecognition = new SpeechRecognition();\n  wakeRecognition.continuous     = true;\n  wakeRecognition.interimResults = true;\n  wakeRecognition.lang           = navigator.language || 'en-US';\n  wakeRecognition.maxAlternatives = 1;\n\n  wakeRecognition.onresult = (event) => {\n    for (let i = event.resultIndex; i < event.results.length; i++) {\n      const transcript = event.results[i][0].transcript.toLowerCase().trim();\n      if (isWakePhrase(transcript)) {\n        handleWakeWordDetected();\n        return;\n      }\n    }\n  };\n\n  wakeRecognition.onerror = (event) => {\n    if (event.error === 'not-allowed' || event.error === 'service-not-allowed') {\n      // Microphone access denied \u2014 silently disable wake mode\n      disableWakeMode();\n      return;\n    }\n    if (wakeMode && !isListening && !wakeTriggered) {\n      scheduleWakeRestart();\n    }\n  };\n\n  wakeRecognition.onend = () => {\n    // Chrome stops continuous recognition periodically \u2014 restart unless we\n    // deliberately stopped it to hand off to main recording.\n    if (wakeMode && !isListening && !wakeTriggered) {\n      scheduleWakeRestart();\n    }\n  };\n}\n\nfunction startWakeRecognition() {\n  if (!wakeRecognition) initWakeRecognition();\n  wakeTriggered = false;\n  quickRing.classList.add('listening-passive'); // passive glow on quick button only\n  try {\n    wakeRecognition.start();\n  } catch (e) {\n    // InvalidStateError when already started \u2014 reinit and retry\n    initWakeRecognition();\n    try { wakeRecognition.start(); } catch (_) {}\n  }\n}\n\nfunction stopWakeRecognition() {\n  quickRing.classList.remove('listening-passive');\n  if (wakeRecognition) {\n    try { wakeRecognition.stop(); } catch (_) {}\n  }\n}\n\nfunction scheduleWakeRestart() {\n  clearTimeout(wakeRestartTimer);\n  wakeRestartTimer = setTimeout(() => {\n    if (wakeMode && !isListening && !wakeTriggered) {\n      startWakeRecognition();\n    }\n  }, 300);\n}\n\nfunction handleWakeWordDetected() {\n  if (isListening || wakeTriggered) return;\n  wakeTriggered = true;\n  wakeTriggeredRecording = true; // flag so finishRecording auto-sends\n  stopWakeRecognition();\n  // Give the recognition engine a moment to fully stop before starting main recording\n  setTimeout(() => {\n    wakeTriggered = false;\n    startListening('quick'); // wake word always triggers quick mode\n  }, 250);\n}\n\nfunction enableWakeMode() {\n  wakeMode = true;\n  wakeBtn.classList.add('wake-active');\n  wakeBtn.setAttribute('aria-pressed', 'true');\n  wakeBtn.setAttribute('aria-label', 'Disable wake word');\n  wakeBtn.title = 'Wake word: ON';\n  localStorage.setItem('wakeMode', '1');\n  updateWakeHint();\n  if (!isListening) startWakeRecognition();\n}\n\nfunction disableWakeMode() {\n  wakeMode = false;\n  wakeBtn.classList.remove('wake-active');\n  wakeBtn.setAttribute('aria-pressed', 'false');\n  wakeBtn.setAttribute('aria-label', 'Enable wake word');\n  wakeBtn.title = 'Wake word: Hey Chill';\n  localStorage.setItem('wakeMode', '0');\n  clearTimeout(wakeRestartTimer);\n  stopWakeRecognition();\n  updateWakeHint();\n}\n\nfunction updateWakeHint() {\n  if (!isListening) {\n    micHint.textContent = wakeMode ? 'Say \"Hey Chill\" or tap Quick' : '';\n    micHint.classList.remove('active', 'brainstorm-active');\n  }\n}\n\nwakeBtn.addEventListener('click', () => {\n  primeAudio();\n  if (wakeMode) {\n    disableWakeMode();\n  } else {\n    enableWakeMode();\n  }\n});\n\n// Restore wake mode preference across sessions\nif (SpeechRecognition && localStorage.getItem('wakeMode') === '1') {\n  enableWakeMode();\n}\n"

Chrome's periodic recognition restarts are handled transparently by accumulating the transcript; user taps again to stop and reviews the full transcript before sending\n\n## Visual distinction\n- Quick uses the existing red/accent gradient + mic icon + red pulse ring\n- Brainstorm uses a purple/accent-2 gradient + waveform-bars icon + purple glow animation\n- Both have text labels (\"Quick\" / \"Brainstorm\") below each button\n- Shared status hint updates to reflect which mode is active\n\n## Key implementation details\n- `activeMode` state (`'quick' | 'brainstorm' | null`) replaces the single implicit mode\n- `resetSilenceTimer` is a no-op in brainstorm mode\n- Brainstorm restart logic: on Chrome's `recognition.onend` mid-session, `brainstormAccumulator` preserves transcript and `_brainstormRestarting` suppresses the `onstart` UI reset\n- Wake word always triggers Quick mode\n\n## Test plan\n- [ ] Quick: tap Quick \u2192 VAD stops after silence \u2192 transcript bar appears \u2192 Send works\n- [ ] Quick: tap Quick \u2192 tap again before silence \u2192 transcript bar appears\n- [ ] Brainstorm: tap Brainstorm \u2192 recording continues past 3.5 s \u2192 tap again \u2192 full transcript shown\n- [ ] Both buttons disabled when SpeechRecognition is unsupported\n- [ ] Tapping one button while the other is recording does nothing\n- [ ] Wake word (\"Hey Chill\") triggers Quick mode, auto-sends\n- [ ] Visual: Quick has red ring when active; Brainstorm has purple ring when active\n\nCloses FRG-211\n\n\ud83e\udd16 Generated with [Claude Code](https://claude.com/claude-code)\nEOF\n)\""

ASSISTANTMESSAGE #78
## Status DONE ## What Changed - `index.html` — replaced single `.mic-ring`/`mic-btn` with two side-by-side buttons: `#quick-btn` (mic icon) and `#brainstorm-btn` (waveform-bars icon), each in a `.mode-btn-wrap` with a label below - `style.css` — added `.mic-buttons` flex container, `.mode-btn-wrap`/`.mode-label` for layout; added `.brainstorm-btn` purple gradient + recording glow animation; scaled both rings/buttons down slightly for side-by-side fit; added `brainstorm-ring.recording` purple ring override - `app.js` — introduced `activeMode` state (`'quick'|'brainstorm'|null`); Quick uses existing VAD silence timer, Brainstorm disables it; seamless Brainstorm restart across Chrome's periodic `onend` using `brainstormAccumulator` + `_brainstormRestarting` flag; updated `setRecordingUI`, `updateWakeHint`, wake-word handlers, and not-supported fallback for two buttons ## Key Decisions - Brainstorm restart preserves accumulated transcript via `brainstormAccumulator` saved in `onend` and restored in `onstart` — avoids a flash/reset of the live transcript area on Chrome's periodic stops - Wake word always triggers Quick mode (a "Hey Chill" utterance is a focused quick request, not an open brainstorm session) - Buttons are sized at 76 px (down from 88 px) to fit comfortably side-by-side on a 360 px mobile screen ## PR / Branch - Branch: `feature/FRG-211-dual-mode-ui-quick-brainstorm` - PR: https://github.com/chillkimtest-oss/hey-chill/pull/5
